   ardhabimbam sarvadā na cakāsti? cakāsti eva | kim iti na upalabhyate?	arDa bimbam sarvadA na cakAsti? cakAsti eva | kim iti naH upalaByate?

   [ candraśṛṅgonnatiḥ ]	[ candra SRFga unnatiH ]

   śapathapratipādanāya āha ã	SapaTa pratipAdanAya Aha ã
   āryabhaṭīyam nāmnā pūrvam svāyambhuvam sadā nityam |	AryaBawI iyam nAmnA pUrvam svAyamBuvam sadA nityam |
   sukṛtāyuṣoḥ praṇāśam kurute pratikañcukam yaḥ asya || 50 ||	sukRta AyuzoH praNASam kurute pratikaQcukam yaH asya || 50 ||
   āryabhaṭasya idam āryabhaṭīyam | kim tat? yadā eva	Arya Bawasya idam Arya BawI iyam | kim tat? yadA eva
   atyantavipralīnasampradāyam brahmaṇaḥ prasādena vā svanāmadheyam | yaḥ	atyanta vipralIna sampradAyam brahmaNaH prasAdena vA sva nAmaDeyam | yaH
   pūrvam svāyambhuvam āsīt idānīm āryabhaṭena prakāśitatvāt āryabhaṭīyam |	pUrvam svAyamBuvam AsIt idAnIm Arya Bawena prakASita tvAt Arya BawI iyam |
   svāyambhuvam tat sarvadā nityam | svayaṃbhuvā praṇītam artham gṛhītvā	svAyamBuvam tat sarvadA nityam | svayaMBuvA praNItam arTam gRhItvA
   ācāryāḥ śāstrāṇi racayanti | sampradāyāvicchedāt tu saḥ arthaḥ jñātaḥ eva	AcAryAH SAstrANi racayanti | sampradAya avicCedAt tu saH arTaH jQAtaH eva
   | anyathā atīndriyārthānām katham mānuṣamātraiḥ iyam yuktiḥ kartum śakyate	| anyaTA atIndriya arTAnAm kaTam mAnuza mAtrEH iyam yuktiH kartum Sakyate
   | asya pratikañcukam	| asya pratikaQcukam
   pratibimbam yaḥ karoti tasya sukṛtasya āyuṣaḥ ca praṇāśam bhavati || 50 ||	pratibimbam yaH karoti tasya sukRtasya AyuzaH ca praNASam Bavati || 50 ||
   [ someśvarabhāṣyasya upasaṃhāraślokaḥ ]	[ someSvara BAzyasya upasaMhAra SlokaH ]
   spaṣṭārthapratipādakam mṛdudhiyām sūktam prabodhapradam	spazwa arTa pratipAdakam mRdu DiyAm sUktam praboDa pradam
   tarkavyākaraṇādiśuddhamatinā someśvareṇa adhunā |	tarka vyAkaraNa Adi SudDa matinA someSvareNa aDunA |
   ācāryāryabhaṭoktasūtravivṛtiḥ yā bhāskarotpāditā	AcArya ArI aBawa ukta sUtra vivRtiH yA BAskara utpAditA
   tasyāḥ sārataram vikṛṣya racitam bhāṣyam prakṛṣṭam laghu ||	tasyAH sArataram vikRzya racitam BAzyam prakRzwam laGu ||
   iti someśvaraviracitam āryabhaṭīyam bhāṣyam samāptam |	iti someSvara viracitam Arya BawI iyam BAzyam samAptam |
   [ bhāskarabhāṣyasya upasaṃhāraślokaḥ ]	[ BAskara BAzyasya upasaMhAraSlokaH ]
   atīndriyārthapratipādakāni	atIndriya arTa pratipAdakAni
   sūtrāṇi amūni āryabhaṭoditāni |	sUtrANi amUni Arya Bawa uditAni |
   teṣām aśakyaḥ arthaśatāṃśakaḥ api	tezAm aSakyaH arTa Sata aMSakaH api
   vaktum kutaḥ asmatsadṛśaiḥ aśeṣam ||	vaktum kutas asmad sadRSEH aSezam ||
   iti bhāskarasya kṛtau āryabhaṭatantrabhāṣye	iti BAskarasya kRtO Arya Bawa tantra BAzye
   golapādaḥ samāptaḥ |	golapAdaH samAptaH |
